06/12/21, 23:50 - Mr. Khandelwal: #include<stdio.h>

int gcd(int val1, int val2)
{
    int temp;
    if(val1 > val2)
    {
        temp = val1;
        val1 = val2;
        val2 = temp;
    }
    if(val2 % val1 == 0)
        return val1;
    else
        return gcdofnumbers(val2 % val1, val1);
}

int lcmofnumbers(int *num1, int *num2)
{
    int gcd = gcdofnumbers(*num1, *num2);
    return ((*num1) * *(num2)) / gcd;
}

int main()
{
    int array[20], count, n, value = 1;
    printf("\nEnter Number of Elements: ");
    scanf("%d", &n);
    printf("\nEnter %d Numbers:\n", n);
    for(count = 0; count < limit; count++)
        scanf("%d", &array[count]);
    for(count = 0; count < limit; count++)
        value = lcmofnumbers(&value, array+count);
    printf("\nLCM of given numbers = %d\n", value);
    return 0;
}

13/12/21, 10:34 - Mr. Khandelwal: #include <stdio.h>

void reverse(char* begin, char* end)
{
	char temp;
	while (begin < end) {
		temp = *begin;
		*begin++ = *end;
		*end-- = temp;
	}
}


void reverseWords(char* s)
{
	char* word_begin = s;

	// Word boundary
	char* temp = s;

	// Reversing individual words as
	// explained in the first step
	while (*temp) {
		temp++;
		if (*temp == '\0') {
			reverse(word_begin, temp - 1);
		}
		else if (*temp == ' ') {
			reverse(word_begin, temp - 1);
			word_begin = temp + 1;
		}
	}


	reverse(s, temp - 1);
}

int main()
{
	char s[] = "SDF-1 Lab Test is very easy .";
	char* temp = s;
	reverseWords(s);
	printf("%s", s);
	return 0;
}

struct info                 //creates structure having information of students
{
    char Name[25];
    long int Rollno;
    char Branch[3];
    int age;
};               //creates array of structure type for 5 students

int* count(struct info* ptr)           //creates function to count students in each branch
{
    int i;
    int a[3]= {0,0,0};              //array to store number of students in each branch
    for(i=0; i<5; i++)
    {
        if(!(strcmp(ptr->Branch, "CSE"))) a[0]++;
        else if(!(strcmp(ptr->Branch, "IT"))) a[1]++;
        else  a[2]++;
        ptr++;
    }
    int *p;
    p=&a[0];
    return p;
}

    char a[5][25];

int main()
{

    struct info students2 = {"Rhythm",10637,"ECE",19};
    struct info students3 = {"Shubham",14617,"CSE",18};
    struct info students4 = {"Jatin",13639,"IT",20};

    ptr=&students1;
    printf("Number of students in CSE : %d\n",*p);
    p++;
    printf("Number of students in IT : %d\n",*p);
    p++;
    printf("Number of students in ECE : %d\n",*p);
    return 0;
}

These 3 Applications are as following :

1.KYC( Know Your Candidate) - ECI dedicated mobile application containing information published by candidates.
Link - https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.eci.ksa

2.cVIGIL -The new cVIGIL app to create a fast-track complaint reception and redressal system. â€˜cVIGILâ€™ stands for Vigilant Citizen and emphasizes the proactive and responsible role citizens can play in the conduct of free and fair elections.
Link - https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=in.nic.eci.cvigil

3.Voter Helpline - Official Election Commission of India App for Voter Registration and Elections.
Link - https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.eci.citizen

using namespace std;
int main()
{
    int n, i;
    cout << "Enter number of students: ";
    cin >> n;
    float *ptr;
    ptr = new float[n];
    cout << "Enter cgpa of students : ";

    {
        cin >> *(ptr + i);
    }
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {

    }
    return 0;
}

	// Write your code here.
	int maxDep=0;
	int counter = 0;
	for(int i=0;i<s.length();i++)
	{
		if(s[i] == '(')
		{
			counter++;
		}
		else if(s[i] == ')')
		{
			counter--;
		}
		else
		{
			maxDep = max(maxDep,counter);
		}
	}
	return maxDep;
}

	int n = s.length();

	int count=0;
	int maxi =0;
	for(int i=n;i>=0;i--)
	{
		if(s[i]==')')
		{
			count++;
		}
		else{
			maxi=max(count,maxi);

		}
	}

	return maxi;
}
19/03/24, 01:48 - Mr. Khandelwal: string longestCommonPrefix(vector<string> &arr, int n)
    {
        // Write your code here
        string result="";
        sort(arr.begin(),arr.end());
        string v1=arr[0];
        string v2 = arr[n-1];
        for(int i=0;i<v1.size();i++)
        {
            if(v1[i]!=v2[i])
            {
                break;
            }
            else{
                result+=v1[i];
            }
        }
        return result;
    }
